		}

				}
			}

						type = arms_factory

					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 77 }
				77 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 80 }
				80 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				}
			}
		}

			factor = 80
		}
	}
